      <p>
       This is a
       <b>
        list of solar eclipses in the 7th century BC
       </b>
       . During the period 700 to 601 BC there were 253
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse" title="Solar eclipse">
        solar eclipses
       </a>
       of which 96 were partial, 87 were annular (one
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse#Terminology" title="Solar eclipse">
        non-central
       </a>
       ), 63 were total, and 7 were hybrids. The greatest number of eclipses in one year was four, occurring in 18 different years: 699 BC, 692 BC, 689 BC, 685 BC, 674 BC, 667 BC, 656 BC, 449 BC, 442 BC, 638 BC, 634 BC, 631 BC, 627 BC, 620 BC, 616 BC, 609 BC, 605 BC, and 602 BC. Three months, December 689 BC, November 678 BC, and October 602 BC, had two eclipses.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nasa_catalog_list_1-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-nasa_catalog_list-1">
         [1]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <div style="clear:both;">
      </div>
